<p>AzureName: The name of the resource in Azure. This is often the same as the name of the resource in Kubernetes but it
doesn&rsquo;t have to be.</p>

</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>

<h3 id="app.azure.com/v1api20240301.AzureActiveDirectoryRegistration">AzureActiveDirectoryRegistration
</h3>
<p>
(<em>Appears on:</em><a href="#app.azure.com/v1api20240301.AzureActiveDirectory">AzureActiveDirectory</a>)
</p>
<div>
<p>The configuration settings of the Azure Active Directory app registration.</p>
</div>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>
<code>clientId</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>ClientId: The Client ID of this relying party application, known as the client_id.
This setting is required for enabling OpenID Connection authentication with Azure Active Directory or
other 3rd party OpenID Connect providers.
More information on OpenID Connect: <a href="http://openid.net/specs/openid-connect-core-1_0.html">http://openid.net/specs/openid-connect-core-1_0.html</a></p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>clientSecretCertificateIssuer</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>ClientSecretCertificateIssuer: An alternative to the client secret thumbprint, that is the issuer of a certificate used
for signing purposes. This property acts as
a replacement for the Client Secret Certificate Thumbprint. It is also optional.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>clientSecretCertificateSubjectAlternativeName</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>ClientSecretCertificateSubjectAlternativeName: An alternative to the client secret thumbprint, that is the subject
alternative name of a certificate used for signing purposes. This property acts as
a replacement for the Client Secret Certificate Thumbprint. It is also optional.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>clientSecretCertificateThumbprint</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>ClientSecretCertificateThumbprint: An alternative to the client secret, that is the thumbprint of a certificate used for
signing purposes. This property acts as
a replacement for the Client Secret. It is also optional.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>clientSecretSettingName</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>ClientSecretSettingName: The app setting name that contains the client secret of the relying party application.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>openIdIssuer</code><br/>
<em>
string
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>OpenIdIssuer: The OpenID Connect Issuer URI that represents the entity which issues access tokens for this application.
When using Azure Active Directory, this value is the URI of the directory tenant, e.g.
<a href="https://login.microsoftonline.com/v2.0/{tenant-guid}/">https://login.microsoftonline.com/v2.0/{tenant-guid}/</a>.
This URI is a case-sensitive identifier for the token issuer.
More information on OpenID Connect Discovery: <a href="http://openid.net/specs/openid-connect-discovery-1_0.html">http://openid.net/specs/openid-connect-discovery-1_0.html</a></p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<h3 id="app.azure.com/v1api20240301.ContainerAppProbe">ContainerAppProbe
</h3>
<p>
(<em>Appears on:</em><a href="#app.azure.com/v1api20240301.Container">Container</a>)
</p>
<div>
<p>Probe describes a health check to be performed against a container to determine whether it is alive or ready to receive
traffic.</p>
</div>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Field</th>
<th>Description</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>
<code>failureThreshold</code><br/>
<em>
int
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>FailureThreshold: Minimum consecutive failures for the probe to be considered failed after having succeeded. Defaults to
3. Minimum value is 1. Maximum value is 10.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>httpGet</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#app.azure.com/v1api20240301.ContainerAppProbe_HttpGet">
ContainerAppProbe_HttpGet
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>HttpGet: HTTPGet specifies the http request to perform.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>initialDelaySeconds</code><br/>
<em>
int
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>InitialDelaySeconds: Number of seconds after the container has started before liveness probes are initiated. Minimum
value is 1. Maximum value is 60.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>periodSeconds</code><br/>
<em>
int
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>PeriodSeconds: How often (in seconds) to perform the probe. Default to 10 seconds. Minimum value is 1. Maximum value is
240.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>successThreshold</code><br/>
<em>
int
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>SuccessThreshold: Minimum consecutive successes for the probe to be considered successful after having failed. Defaults
to 1. Must be 1 for liveness and startup. Minimum value is 1. Maximum value is 10.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>tcpSocket</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#app.azure.com/v1api20240301.ContainerAppProbe_TcpSocket">
ContainerAppProbe_TcpSocket
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>TcpSocket: TCPSocket specifies an action involving a TCP port. TCP hooks not yet supported.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>terminationGracePeriodSeconds</code><br/>
<em>
int
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>TerminationGracePeriodSeconds: Optional duration in seconds the pod needs to terminate gracefully upon probe failure.
The grace period is the duration in seconds after the processes running in the pod are sent a termination signal and the
time when the processes are forcibly halted with a kill signal. Set this value longer than the expected cleanup time for
your process. If this value is nil, the pod&rsquo;s terminationGracePeriodSeconds will be used. Otherwise, this value
overrides the value provided by the pod spec. Value must be non-negative integer. The value zero indicates stop
immediately via the kill signal (no opportunity to shut down). This is an alpha field and requires enabling
ProbeTerminationGracePeriod feature gate. Maximum value is 3600 seconds (1 hour)</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>timeoutSeconds</code><br/>
<em>
int
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>TimeoutSeconds: Number of seconds after which the probe times out. Defaults to 1 second. Minimum value is 1. Maximum
value is 240.</p>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>
<code>type</code><br/>
<em>
<a href="#app.azure.com/v1api20240301.ContainerAppProbe_Type">
ContainerAppProbe_Type
</a>
</em>
</td>
<td>
<p>Type: The type of probe.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<code>true</code>.</p>
</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

bool
</em>
</td>

string
</em>

<em>
string
</em>
</td>

internal DNS server.</p>
</td>
</tr>

<p>MaximumCount: The maximum capacity.</p>
</td>
</tr>
